Larchmont Village is a quaint and friendly shopping district in the center of a bustling city. It is located in one of the oldest and most historically significant neighborhoods in Los Angeles and is bordered by some of the most well preserved older homes in the city, ranging from 1920's California bungalows to grand old estates. Larchmont Village serves as a Main Street retail district to Hancock Park, Windsor Square and nearby Paramount Studios. Larchmont maintains a small town feel and serves as a lovely community gathering place. Enjoy the charm of a day spent on Larchmont experiencing a variety of wonderful ethnic restaurants, sidewalk cafes and upscale boutiques. Hancock Park is approximately 2.2 square miles and consists of about 1,200 homes. Its boundaries are Rossmore to Highland Avenues, and Melrose Avenue to Wilshire Boulevard. This is rate the #1 safest neighborhood in Los Angeles. There is parking in the driveway and on the street.

Closest to the Thai Town part of Hollywood, the neighborhood is mixed residential - some single family homes, some newer condos and apartment buildings. Walk a couple blocks and you're on a retail street close to bus service. It's very central, super close to both K-Town and the more nightlife-y parts of Hollywood. The only thing that's a little tricky is parking, but if you're familiar with LA you'll expect that - it's the trade off you get for being so central - and it's easier than parking in K-Town or downtown. I was always able to find something no more than a couple blocks away, and sometimes, depending on the time of day, I ended up right in front.                         Available for month to month (or longer) bookings, Great for a family or large group, the house is pretty private and has plenty of space for everyone. Three full bedrooms + bonus room w/ futon + living room queen size pull-out couch bed. Fresh towels and sheets for every stay are provided. Big TV projector in the living room is perfect for getting together and watching movies. Comes with free fast WiFi and parking spot easy street parking!

                       <div data-reactid="3">
                        Here is a more detailed description of the property! If you have any questions at all, feel free to shoot me an e-mail to ask. This is a private home located in an hip neighborhood in Hollywood. It's great for groups and families traveling together. Lots of light, very spacious and in a fantastic location in the middle of LA. The house is charming but spacious, I did a lot of the craftsman work myself! When you walk in, you enter in the bonus room. This room has a TV (hooked up to a Netflix and Hulu) and a couch futon that can be used as a bed. It has it's own door and closet. After entering into the bonus room, you walk into the living room. It is very large and has two couches. The best part about the living room is that has a projector TV (also hooked up to a separate Netflix and Hulu). Great for group gatherings and hanging out in. As you walk down the hallway towards the rest of the house, you have one bedroom to the left and one to the right. The bedroom on the left has a sliding glass door, the one on the right has a full door. They both have very large comfortable queen beds. As you continue down the hallways there is a full bathroom to the right, which has as shower and cabinet space. It's the green marble one you see in the picture. Past the bathroom on the left is the kitchen and ahead of you is the master bedroom. The kitchen is quite large and has seating for 6 people + additional stools if you need them. Great to cook in and open floor plan so you can cook and sit at the table at the same time. The master bedroom has it's own half bath and seating area, en suite. It also has a large closet and plenty of drawers and cabinet space. Fresh linens, towels, sheets are provided and so are all of your basic household amenities: pots, pans, microwave, stove, utensils, plates, shampoo, soap...I think that's everything but feel free to ask if there is something in particular you are curious about. Every bedroom pretty much has it's own in window AC unit, but the house itself is actually pretty well insulated so heat isn't really a problem.
                       </div>

The area is very conveniently located in Los Angeles: 5 Minutes to the Hollywood and Highland 10 Minutes from the Grove / West Hollywood 15 Minutes from Beverly Hills 20 Minutes from LAX or Downtown LA 25 Minutes to Santa Monica Beach and Venice Beach

                      <div data-reactroot="" data-reactid="1" data-react-checksum="-502187799">
                       <div data-reactid="2">
                        This beautiful Spanish home is nestled in the famous old Hollywood neighborhood of Hancock Park, centrally located between Beverly Hills &amp; Downtown, 2 miles south of Hollywood &amp; Vine, walking distance from quaint Larchmont Blvd &amp; Paramount Studios.
                       </div>
                       <div data-reactid="3">
                        If location is important to you, it doesn't get better than this. This classic Spanish style 3 bed 2 1/2 bathroom Hancock Park private home is walking distance from Paramount Studios, 2 miles from famed Hollywood &amp; Vine, and close to freeways 10 and 101. This very central neighborhood is 4.5 miles from Beverly Hills' Rodeo Drive in one direction and 5 miles from Downtown Los Angeles in the other. Only two blocks away, a 5 min walk, is the very popular Larchmont Blvd, a quaint street with stores, all kinds of restaurants (vegetarian, greek, italian, sushi, deli, etc.) and all three different popular coffee chains, not to mention a bakery and a couple of frozen yogurt stores. The Hancock Park neighborhood is classic old Hollywood, filled with dramatic mansions that go back to the 1920s. This is the neighborhood where Prince William and Kate stay when they visit California, and where Antonio Banderas and Melanie Griffith call home when not in Spain. Downstairs is a large living room with dramatic fireplace, a family room with 52" plasma television, long antique dinning room table that seats 8, a full restaurant style kitchen with Wolf stove, and a small bathroom (toilet and sink only). This is a family home, so upstairs you'll find a large master bedroom with a cal-king bed and private bathroom with separate shower and bathtub tiled in slate. Two other smaller kid bedrooms share a second bathroom (shower, toilet and sink, no bathtub), and also share a large patio/sun deck. The bigger of the two has a queen size bed, the smaller a full size bed. Amenities include cable TV with HBO, internet, plus washer &amp; dryer. Outside there is a private sitting area with water fountain and outdoor fireplace (great for entertaining), off street parking for 2 vehicles, plus plenty of street parking. There is a 5 night minimum stay. Now for the rules: This is a family neighborhood, it is very safe and quiet. We would like to keep it that way. This is NOT a party house. Also, no professional photography or filming allowed. This house is listed with a location rental agencie, and the rates for that kind of use are very different. Last but not least, there is no smoking allowed inside the home. There is a smoking area by the outside fireplace. Thank you for understanding.
                       </div>

It is located in one of the oldest and most historically significant neighborhoods in Los Angeles and is bordered by some of the most well preserved older homes in the city, ranging from 1920's California bungalows to grand old estates. Larchmont Village serves as a Main Street retail district to Hancock Park, Windsor Square and nearby Paramount Studios. Larchmont maintains a small town feel and serves as a lovely community gathering place. Enjoy the charm of a day spent on Larchmont experiencing a variety of wonderful ethnic restaurants, sidewalk cafes and upscale boutiques. Hancock Park is approximately 2.2 square miles and consists of about 1,200 homes. Its boundaries are Rossmore to Highland Avenues, and Melrose Avenue to Wilshire Boulevard. This is rate the #1 safest neighborhood in Los Angeles. There is parking in the driveway and on the street.

                       <div data-reactid="4">
                        This area is a well-kept secret in the heart of the city. Hancock Park is a very unique neighborhood and in this city of cars, it is a joy to be in a neighborhood such as this one where you can walk to Larchmont Village, a jewel in the heart of the city. You can also walk to museums, theaters, the heart of Hollywood, and to buses and metros. You may find less expensive lodgings in what seems like a neighborhood close to this one, but beware that neighborhoods in LA change dramatically within the span of a few blocks. My house is a very short walk to Larchmont village : Walk to it for cafes, shops and restaurants... always full of actors and film writers because Paramount Studios is just down the street. Lots of great restaurants to walk to. Many places to get coffee, pastries, ice cream, etc. You will be in the heart of the city where Hollywood is up the street, and Santa Monica beach is a mere twenty minute drive. Downtown and Beverly Hills are both close by, as are the theater row, museums, movie houses and lots more.
